## 📝 Recommendations for Manual Review

### Priority Order for Manual Review:

1. **🔥 CRITICAL (5+ steps):** Review immediately - these severely impact progression
2. **🔴 HIGH (4 steps):** Review soon - significant complexity
3. **🟡 MODERATE (3 steps):** Review when possible - manageable complexity

### Specific Actions:

- **For T1-T2 components:** Find simpler alternatives or break into smaller components
- **For T3-T4 components:** Consider if complexity is justified for mid-game
- **For T5 components:** Generally acceptable but review if used in critical early buildings
- **Infrastructure buildings:** Can handle more complex components
- **Resource extraction buildings:** Should prioritize simpler components for early tiers

### Questions to Ask During Manual Review:

1. Is this component used in any T1-T3 resource buildings?
2. Can this component be broken down into simpler sub-components?
3. Are there existing simpler alternatives that could be used instead?
4. Is the complexity justified by the component's function and tier?
5. Would replacing this component improve early-game progression?
